niceGs:=[S^-i*r[1]*S^i: i in [0..q-1]];
//test
    test:=procedure(niceGs, G, ind)
        ind2:=Index(G, sub<G|niceGs>);
        if ind eq ind2 then//correct index
            if IsNormal(G, sub<G|niceGs>) then//normal
                f,Q:=CosetAction(G, sub<G|niceGs>);
                if [Order(f(w)): w in [R*S, R, S]] eq [2,p,q] then//torsion free
                    print #niceGs-2*g;//number of excess generators
                else
                    print "not torsion free";
                end if;
            else 
                print "not normal";
            end if;
        else
            print "wrong index:", ind2;
        end if;
    end procedure;
test(niceGs, G, ind);
#r;

//find labels
    L:=CosGraphLabs(G, niceGs);
    getConjLabs(L,G, niceGs, [R,S,R*S]);
    getLabs(L,G, niceGs, r);

//Get rels if labels are too long
    getRels(G,niceGs);

//if generating set can't be found
    //get normal subgroups
    L1:=LowIndexNormalSubgroups(G, ind);

    //get torsion free subgroups of correct index
    L2:=[];
    for i in [1..#L1] do
        if L1[i]`Index eq ind then
            f,Q:=CosetAction(G, L1[i]`Group);
            if [Order(f(w)): w in [R*S, R, S]] eq [2,p,q] then
                Append(~L2, L1[i]);
            end if;
        end if;
    end for;
    #L2;
    L2;

        >     getLabs(L,G, niceGs, r);
